<review>I have read the previous reviews and they all say Banfield is expensive and they do tend to be on the pricey side which is why I only gave them 4 stars. I have taken pets there for a least 13 years. I did have one pet die in surgery but the dog had a perforated bowel and the Vet was in tears when the dog could not be saved. It was not the Vet's fault. I have been there for a severe bee sting reaction, neutering, ear infection, eye injury etc. The receptionist is beyond kind and always helpful. The vet. assistants are the same. The vet I see, Dr. Orth is fantastic and I would trust her with my pets any day. <rating>5<//rating>< Text>
Came here with my Husband, whose review is below. Most gun shops are about the same, to me, with fairly general stock and pretty standard solemn faced people. Not this place. They have a pretty fantastic variety of guns and we even found the clips we were looking for that we couldn't find anywhere else (that wasn't online). There are some really interesting and novel pieces around the store as well.
The folks are very friendly and pleasant, they're extremely fun to talk to, and reasonably knowledgeable. Filling out the paperwork for my Marlin was a breeze and took barely any time at all. I actually really like their selection of rifle bags much better than large chain stores. They seem to be of higher quality and the prices are comparable, some even better than.
The overall setup of the store is nice and expansive, open and comfortable, yet doesn't have that "bare shelf" feel you can get at similar places.
Overall I definitely recommend stopping by. It's a trek from where we are, but we'll be back. It's worth the drive.</Text>

<Rating>1</Rating>< Review>
The question is not if, but when a tragedy involving a child or children will occur in the parking lot near the entrance of Calphin Aquatic Club in Fremont if one has not occurred already. I have witnessed young excited swimmers darting to-and-from the tanks as parent drivers and Motel 6 guests speed to-and-from the facilities seemingly without any regard to the safety of the youth. There are also vehicles backing blindly out of parking spaces. What a recipe for disaster exists here at Calphin Aquatic Club. There should be serious safety instructon for the parents and children regarding this dangerous condition. Responsible authorative safety spotters should be stationed outside the entrance of this pool building at all times during busy hours just like the lifeguards must standby the pools. The ignored "Student Crossing" sign should be at least 4x8 feet in size and well lit for the even worse situation after sunset. I am helping out with a large estate, and I have been a long-term Motel 6 guest. My one star rating is not based on the quality of the swimming program, but on the apparent failure of pool management to solve this spine-tingling hazard placing children at a very scary safety risk. What a poorly engineered facility entrance that should be on the opposite side of the structure with a mandatory safe supervised pick-up and drop-off zone away from the vehicle traffic flow. If a fatality has not occurred, then a miracle is in progress at this location. But something must be done immediately so blood is not on the hands of pool management one day and the directors will not have to live on with the horrible remorse for the remainder of their respective lives.
Please take my concerns in a positive spirit as from where I sit it certainly appears you might have a great program at Calphin Aquatic Club!!!

Jeff,
Salem-Silverton, Oregon< /Review>

I am currently 5 months pregnant and was extremely worried about a dentist still pushing X-rays so was very careful in where I chose to go. After reading many, many reviews and asking for recommendations on the local Facebook group, Hada Family Dental was recommended and I decided to schedule. In addition to me being pregnant, I am also diagnosed with Hyperemesis gravidarum. HG is a pregnancy complication that is characterized by severe nausea, vomiting, weight loss, and possibly dehydration. Feeling faint may also occur so I was very worried about a simple teeth cleaning as I cannot even hold water down at this moment. Upon checking in, I threw up 3 times in the bathroom and was worried I might have to reschedule. The staff advised me that ironically, 5 of the staff are pregnant including my dental hygienist, Cori Salazar, RDH. It made me feel more comfortable regarding my care so I moved forward with the appointment and it was truly the best experience I could've had given my situation. I think I was a hard patient as my nausea was constant and I had to keep getting up to take a minute so I don't throw up, but Cori was absolutely nothing less than exemplary. She was so professional, so courteous and so understanding that I was in utter disbelief. She took her time cleaning my teeth and let me take as many breaks as possible, even if that meant keeping me after they close. She even offered to split the cleaning appointment into two if it was too much for me to handle at once. I have never received such amazing service as this in my life. Not to mention, I was provided with a business card to call at any time I needed to, even after hours, in case I had any concerns at all. Now that is service that I will keep coming back for. My husband and son will be coming in for an appointment soon and I am very confident that we will be lifetime clients of Hada Family Dental. Superb experience!<//text>

< review>
If you want to go to a dental practice that takes care of you from the moment you walk through the door this is your place. All the staff (front office, RDA's, RDH's) are all so friendly and have ample experience so you know you're in good hands. Of course the owner, Dr. Hada, who is a family friend, is an exceptional Dentist!

Today for example I got an old silver filling taken out and it was replaced with white composite. Eber, the RDA, was very nice and numbed my gums prior to the maxillary nerve block shot. When Dr. Hada went in with the shot I didn't feel a thing! This is mostly due to the fact that he took his time to slowly release the numbing agent. I appreciated him putting my comfort level as a priority, most dentists probably wouldn't have taken the time to do that since they have many patients to see. He also walked me through what he was doing and made sure I was comfortable during the whole procedure. Its little things like that that make a huge difference in a dental visit. I am already looking forward to my next cleaning.

Call and make an appointment today, you will not regret it!< /review>
